    WHEN [t0].[Id] IS NOT NULL THEN COALESCE([t0].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([t0].[LastName], N'')
    ELSE NULL

    FROM [Students] AS [s]
    WHERE [t].[Id] = [s].[ClassId]) AS [StudentCount]

    FROM [Classes] AS [c]
